                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>Superlative degree এর ক্ষেত্রে 'most' word দ্বারা যখন 'very' বা খুব বেশি বোঝায়, তখন&nbsp;the এর পরিবর্তে a বসে।</p>

border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 5.652em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></msub><mo>∝</mo><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mo>∝</mo><msqrt><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></msub></msqrt><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>1</mn></msub><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mfrac><mo>=</mo><msqrt><mfrac><msub><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></msub></mrow><mn>1</mn></msub><msub><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></msub></mrow><mn>2</mn></msub></mfrac></msqrt><mo>=</mo><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><msqrt><mfrac><msub><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></msub></mrow><mn>1</mn></msub><mrow><mn>4</mn><msub><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">E</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">k</mi></msub></mrow><mn>1</mn></msub></mrow></mfrac></msqrt><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mo>∴</mo><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>2</mn></msub><mo>=</mo><mn>2</mn><msub><mi mathvariant="normal">P</mi><mn>1</mn></msub></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-23">\rm E_k\propto P^2 \Rightarrow P\propto\sqrt{E_k} \\ \Rightarrow\frac{P_1}{P_2}=\sqrt{\frac{{E_k}_1}{{E_k}_2}}=\ \sqrt{\frac{{E_k}_1}{4{E_k}_1}}=\frac{1}{2} \\ \therefore P_2=2P_1&nbsp;</script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৩৫৩]</p>

                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 47</span></div>

width: 0px; height: 1.068em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.647em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 2.002em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mfrac><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi><mi class="MJX-variant" mathvariant="normal">′</mi></msup><mi mathvariant="normal">g</mi></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">h</mi></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>−</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">h</mi></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">h</mi></mrow><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mn>2</mn></mfrac><mo stretchy="false">⇒</mo><mtext>&nbsp;</mtext><mi mathvariant="normal">h</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mi mathvariant="normal">R</mi><mn>4</mn></mfrac></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-38">\rm \frac{g^\prime}{g}=1-\frac{2h}{R}\Rightarrow\frac{1}{2}=1-\frac{2h}{R}\Rightarrow\frac{2h}{R}=\frac{1}{2}&nbsp;
\Rightarrow\ h=\frac{R}{4}</script></span><br>
[ইসহাক স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-৪২৩]</p>
</span>
                                    </div>
                            </div>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>(n+l) এর নিয়মানুযায়ী,&nbsp;<br>
4s=4+0=4&nbsp;<br>
3d=3+2=5 &nbsp;<br>
4p=4+1=5&nbsp;<br>
∴ শক্তিক্রম : 4s&lt;3d&lt;4p<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১২৪]</p>
</span>

                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>‘g’ উপশক্তিস্তরে l = 4;<br>
<span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-48-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>&amp;#x2234;</mo></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-654" style="width: 0.658em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 0.535em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.6em, 1000.49em, 2.379em, -999.998em); top: -2.17em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-655"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-656" style="font-family: MathJax_AMS;">∴</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 2.174em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.148em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 0.753em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>∴</mo></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-48">\rm \therefore</script></span> মোট অরবিটাল সংখ্যা <span class="math-tex"><span class="MathJax_Preview" style="color: inherit; display: none;"></span><span class="MathJax" id="MathJax-Element-49-Frame" tabindex="0" style="position: relative;" data-mathml="<math xmlns=&quot;http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML&quot;><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>(</mo><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant=&quot;normal&quot;>l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>&amp;#x00D7;</mo><mn>4</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy=&quot;false&quot;>)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>9</mn></math>" role="presentation"><nobr aria-hidden="true"><span class="math" id="MathJax-Span-657" style="width: 12.215em; display: inline-block;"><span style="display: inline-block; position: relative; width: 10.002em; height: 0px; font-size: 122%;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(1.109em, 1009.96em, 2.338em, -999.998em); top: -1.965em; left: 0em;"><span class="mrow" id="MathJax-Span-658"><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-659" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">=</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-660" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">(</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-661" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-662" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">l</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-663" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">+</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-664" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">1</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-665" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-666" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-667" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">(</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-668" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">2</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-669" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">×</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-670" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">4</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-671" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">+</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-672" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.207em;">1</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-673" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">)</span><span class="mo" id="MathJax-Span-674" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">=</span><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-675" style="font-family: MathJax_Main; padding-left: 0.289em;">9</span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.348em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.302em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mi mathvariant="normal">l</mi><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>2</mn><mo>×</mo><mn>4</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mn>9</mn></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-49">\rm =(2l+1)=(2\times4+1)= 9</script></span> টি।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১০৩]</p>

                                    <div class="row">
                                        <div class="serial"><span>Question 90</span></div>
                                        <div class="questionText" style="display: block;">
                                            <p>উচ্চ শক্তিস্তর থেকে ২য় শক্তিস্তরে আসলে কোন বর্ণালি সৃষ্টি হয়?</p>

                                    </div>
                                </div>
                                <div class="row questionOptions">
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group " style="align-items: center;">
                                            <div class="input-group-prepend">
                                                <span class="input-group-text">A</span>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>বামার</p>
</label>

                                                <label style="margin-left:5px;"><p>ফুন্&zwnj;ড</p>
</label>
                                                
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    </div>
                                    <div class="col-sm-12 row questionOption">
                                        <div class="input-group " style="align-items: center;">

                                                <span class="input-group-text">C</span>

</label>
                                                
                                            </div>

                                    </div>

</label>

                                    </div>

                                    <div class="row solveText" style="display: block; padding:10px; color:#077307; overflow-x: auto; background-color: #d7f7d4;">
                                        <span style="color: black !important; font-weight: bold;">Solution:</span>
                                        <br>
                                        <span style="color: black !important;"><p>জেনে রাখো: উচ্চ শক্তিস্তর হতে প্রথম শক্তিস্তরে&nbsp;আসলে লাইমেন সিরিজ;<br>
উচ্চ শক্তিস্তর হতে ৩য় শক্তিস্তরে&nbsp;আসলে প্যাশ্চেন সিরিজ;<br>
উচ্চ শক্তিস্তর হতে ৪র্থ শক্তিস্তরে&nbsp;আসলে ব্রাকেট সিরিজ;<br>
উচ্চ শক্তিস্তর হতে ৫ম শক্তিস্তরে&nbsp;আসলে ফুন্&zwnj;ড&nbsp;সিরিজ।<br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১৪৪]</p>
</span>

position: relative; width: 0.986em; height: 0px;"><span style="position: absolute; clip: rect(3.199em, 1000.49em, 4.182em, -999.998em); top: -4.014em; left: 0em;"><span class="mi" id="MathJax-Span-1197" style="font-family: MathJax_Main;">S</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span><span style="position: absolute; top: -4.383em; left: 0.576em;"><span class="mn" id="MathJax-Span-1198" style="font-size: 70.7%; font-family: MathJax_Main;">3</span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 4.018em;"></span></span></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; width: 0px; height: 1.969em;"></span></span></span><span style="display: inline-block; overflow: hidden; vertical-align: -0.348em; border-left: 0px solid; width: 0px; height: 1.552em;"></span></span></nobr><span class="MJX_Assistive_MathML" role="presentation"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML"><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi></msup><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">y</mi><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi></msup><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mi mathvariant="normal">x</mi><mo>+</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">y</mi></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><msup><mn>2</mn><mn>2</mn></msup><msup><mn>.1</mn><mn>1</mn></msup><msup><mrow><mo>(</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mo>)</mo></mrow><mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD"><mn>2</mn><mo>+</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow></msup><mo>=</mo><mn>4</mn><msup><mi mathvariant="normal">S</mi><mn>3</mn></msup></math></span></span><script type="math/tex" id="MathJax-Element-89">\rm x^xy^xS^{x+y}=2^2.1^1\left(S\right)^{2+1}=4S^3&nbsp;</script></span><br>
[হাজারী স্যার: সংস্করণ-২০২২, পৃষ্ঠা-১৭০]</p>
